### Round 8: Austrian Grand Prix
*Date: 2015-06-21*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 16: United States Grand Prix
*Date: 2015-10-25*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
